Commentary

Concern for Secondary Education 83

— Ru

All parents with young children studying in secondary schools are concerned about secondary education. Parents usually expect their children to study hard and warn them against idleness. But at this time, they are worried about their studies. When asked what they are troubled by, they say that the workload is too heavy or the curriculum is not suitable.

Junior high schools have 34 to 35 hours of lessons per week. Someone estimated that it is 12 or 13 hours more than the fourth grade of French middle schools, and 5 or 6 hours more than the third grade of German academic high schools. Senior high schools have 31 to 34 hours of lessons per week. This is 8 to 11 hours more than the philosophy grade of French middle schools, and 2 to 5 hours more than the first grade of German academic high schools. The rigorous cultivation of French and German middle schools is world-renowned, but the homework in our country's middle schools is even heavier. Combining lesson time and self-study time at school, junior high school students work 48 hours per week, and senior high school students work 60 hours per week. In addition, the monthly exams, term exams, and entrance exams create constant fear and extreme tension. Leaving aside life education and production education, the question of whether this book knowledge can be absorbed and integrated calmly is also doubtful. Even more, it affects the physical and mental development of young people and indirectly affects the future health of the nation.

Senior high school courses once adopted a system of dividing subjects and elective subjects. In recent years, due to the needs of university admissions, it has been said that it is appropriate to improve the level, reversing what was done before. Senior high school students, regardless of gender, whether they go to college or not, and regardless of whether those who go to college study liberal arts, law, commerce, science, engineering, or medicine, are all given a fixed and uniform curriculum. Among them, mathematics, in particular, requires all students to study algebra, geometry, trigonometry, and an outline of analytic geometry, which is feared by most young people. When their level is measured, the entrance exam scores are still the worst in mathematics. After all, people's minds are different, and no exam can force them to be the same. Those who discuss it also quote European middle schools as models, criticizing the system of dividing subjects, believing that it is merely imitating the superficial aspects of American education, and ignoring the fact that the decline in the level of middle schools is related to teachers, teaching materials, methods, equipment, and even the entire academic atmosphere. It is by no means a single issue of dividing subjects. If we must compare it with European and American middle schools, according to what we know for sure, the preparatory middle schools for college admissions in Europe have more divisions of schools, classes, and groups than American middle schools, which only divide subjects by college admissions and occupation. The methods of middle schools in various countries are recorded in documents and are visible to everyone. It is not difficult to review them. Moreover, the simple principle of teaching according to aptitude does not require detailed examination of precedents and then proof. However, the opinions of the education community have diverged so much in the past ten years, which is puzzling.

Recently, the Ministry of Education formulated the outline of the method for provincial and municipal secondary normal education research associations, ordering all provinces and cities to establish research associations immediately, and limiting the reporting of research results to the ministry before the end of May. We firmly believe that middle school principals and education experts who participate in this important meeting will be able to study fairly and according to what is appropriate, and not take their personal preferences as public right and wrong. Then, the future of youth education will be fortunate.

Page 7

A Great Threat to World Peace: Germany Begins Rearmament; Compulsory Military Service Implemented Yesterday; Massive Production of Military Supplies and Aircraft; Able to Fight in Less Than a Year 84

(Geneva) Germany will have sufficient strength by March next year and will be able to cope with a major war. This alarming news was released to the Associated Press today by senior military advisers from member states of the League of Nations. It is reported that the German government has been manufacturing massive amounts of war materials since October last year. This manufacturing plan can be completed within 16 to 17 months. Most military experts estimate that Germany already has 3,300 aircraft, pilots say so, while Britain only has 2,200 and France has no more than 5,000. French officials said that although Germany currently lacks large bombers, it is rapidly manufacturing them in large quantities, and their quality is superior to that of aircraft from other countries. It is also heard that the German Ministry of the Army had long planned to manufacture the latest weapons, the root models of which have been destroyed, but the drawings are carefully preserved for future reference. Until October last year, when Supreme Leader Hitler ordered the start of manufacturing, the whole country worked together. By March next year, it will be sufficient for the application of the new German army, and there will be a lot of preparation. Yesterday, although the German Embassy in the UK denied that the German air force was not superior to the British, it was also equal to the British. Some military aspects do not believe this statement. (1st - National Telegram)

Methods of Implementing Compulsory Military Service

(Berlin) Germany's move to expand its army in violation of the peace treaty is scheduled to begin today. According to current estimates, Germany has a total of 750,000 troops. According to reliable sources, the implementation methods of the compulsory military service system are as follows: a total of 580,000 people in the 1915 class will be convened today, of which 300,000 will enter the camp for service. As for the classes from 1901 to 1909, they will receive short-term military training in the coming years, no more than eight weeks each time. The 1901 class will be convened on October 1 this year, and the second batch will be convened on April 1 next year. It is heard that the selection is very strict, and special consideration will be given to married people and professional talents. Preparations such as the accommodation of new recruits are being actively carried out. A new national defense law will be announced soon to establish a national defense administrative committee. Generals Ludendorff and Seeckt, famous during the European War, will be powerful figures in this committee. The Minister of Finance is racking his brains to find a way to balance the budget because the funds needed by the army and navy are huge. At the same time, in order to keep Germany moving forward, a special law has now been promulgated authorizing the Minister of Finance to assume certain guarantees, such as raising 200 million marks to promote German export trade, raising 100 million marks to increase funding for more work, and raising 88 million marks for agricultural funding. (1st - Reuters)

Total Military Strength Reaches 9 Million

(Berlin) According to military sources, the total number of German troops, excluding those who participated in the European War, is about 9 million. Those engaged in compulsory labor service will be the preliminary preparation for military service. All classes from 1901 to 1915 must be conscripted. Among them, those from 1901 to 1909 should receive eight weeks of military training, and those from 1910 to 1915 should receive six months or one year of training. Therefore, Germany's military strength is as follows: (1) The National Defense Force, in principle, has 100,000 professional soldiers; (2) The professional soldiers recruited from the Green Shirts and Black Shirts Guards under the Air Minister Goering, the total number of which is more than 100,000; (3) New recruits recruited from various classes, of which there are about 600,000 in the 1915 class, about 400,000 in the 1916 class, about 350,000 in the 1917 class, and about 300,000 in the 1918 class. Therefore, the issue of military quotas is not difficult to solve in terms of numbers.

National Finance Adds Heavy Burden

However, in terms of finance, there are still many difficulties. Every German conscripted into the army must be paid 40 pfennigs per day, and his wife will be given 45 marks of alimony per month. In addition, children's education expenses and housing funds are not included. Therefore, every conscripted soldier inevitably increases the country's huge burden. According to the former Minister of National Defense, General Xue Kede, the principle of establishing a professional commando team and supplementing it with conscription has been abandoned by the government and the principle of compulsory military service has been adopted. In theory, this principle should make the whole country a soldier, but in practice, the professional army will still only be 200,000 in a few years, but in addition, it will increase the conscription quota.

General Staff Formally Restored

The newly promulgated law stipulates the restoration of the General Staff (according to the Treaty of Versailles, Germany is prohibited from establishing a General Staff). Former Chief of Staff Ludendorff has officially resumed his original position. In addition, the Supreme Military Conference is jointly organized by representatives of the army and navy. General Seeckt, who is now assisting General Chiang Kai-shek in suppressing bandits in China, will also return to China to participate in the Supreme Military Conference. (1st - Havas)

Supreme Leader's Spokesperson Declares to the Outside World

Goebbels, Minister of Propaganda of Germany, recently made a declaration here in Karlsruhe, Germany, saying, "We will never threaten other countries, but we cannot tolerate the threats of other countries. Our country has now become a sovereign and complete country again. Germany does not think of war. Those who say that Germany is engaged in war must be villains who speak too much and must lose. The world says that Germany demands a part of the Polish corridor and the territory of the Czech Republic and Austria, as well as Alsace-Lorraine and other territories, which are completely forged. Foreign newspapers publish this kind of false news, which is enough to disrupt world peace. I hope that the people of the world will respect each other in order to lay the foundation of peace. Germany will naturally work for this kind of peace, and German athletes are willing to dedicate themselves to peace." (31st - Havas)

Anglo-Russian Joint Declaration: Willing to Cooperate to Promote Peace; Clarification of the Purpose of the East European Security Organization: Not to Encircle or Isolate Any Country 85

(Moscow) British Lord Privy Seal Anthony Eden came here to discuss with the Soviet Russian authorities the European crisis caused by Germany's decision to rearm. He has obtained a promise from the Russian authorities to cooperate with Britain in seeking peace. After the meeting, a communique was issued, stating that Britain and Russia are willing to cooperate to seek peace. The text stated that the talks between the two sides involved major events in the current international situation, such as the East European Pact and the matters mentioned in the Anglo-French communique of February 3. (Note: The Anglo-French communique stated the need to maintain the independence and integrity of Austria, advocated inviting Germany to cooperate, opposed unilateral actions to deny international obligations, welcomed the conclusion of a European mutual assistance pact, suggested replacing the military restrictions imposed on Germany by the Treaty of Versailles with an agreement, Germany's return to the League of Nations, and the conclusion of an air pact.)

Talks Between Both Sides: Sincere and Friendly

Eden and Litvinov also discussed the future development and enhancement of Anglo-Russian relations. Eden also exchanged views on this issue with Stalin and Molotov. The talks between the two sides were conducted in an atmosphere of friendship and sincerity throughout. Eden informed Litvinov of the situation of the Anglo-German talks in Berlin. Both sides believed that such talks would help clarify the overall situation in Europe.

Collective Security: A Matter of Utmost Urgency

Eden, Litvinov, Stalin, and Molotov also believed that in the current international situation, it is a matter of utmost urgency to strive to create a system of European collective security as mentioned in the Anglo-French communique of February 3, in accordance with the principles of the League of Nations. Stalin, Molotov, and Litvinov also earnestly stated that the organization of East European security and the conclusion of mutual assistance pacts are not intended to encircle any country or isolate it. They are intended to create equal security for participating countries, and therefore welcome the participation of Germany and Poland, as this would provide the most satisfactory solution to the problem.

Anglo-Russian Interests: No Conflict

After a sincere exchange of views, the representatives of the British and Russian governments recognized that there are currently no conflicts of interest between the two governments on any major issues of international policy. This is a solid foundation for the two countries to cooperate sincerely in seeking peace. They also believe that since both countries recognize that peace can benefit both sides, they will naturally govern their mutual relations in a spirit of cooperation and loyalty to their obligations as members of the League of Nations. In view of these reasons, Eden, Stalin, Molotov, and Litvinov affirmed that they hold the same view and feel that the two countries working together in a friendly spirit to manage the general work of the organization of peace and security blocs is the first and most important step in promoting international efforts to achieve this goal. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

(Moscow) Regarding the section in the communique hoping that Germany and Poland would participate in the East European Mutual Assistance Pact, Soviet Russian officials stated that the so-called "best solution" does not mean that the participation of Germany and Poland is the only solution. It is now known that the above-mentioned communique was originally scheduled to be announced at 6:00 PM (Russian time), but it was delayed because Eden wanted to consult the British government for approval. It was later learned that after the reply telegram from London arrived, Maisky (Soviet Ambassador to the United Kingdom) made several trips back and forth between the Foreign Affairs Committee and the British Embassy before the wording of the communique was finalized. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

Enhanced Diplomatic Relations: A Clear Symbol

(London) The foreign affairs correspondent of the Daily Telegraph attaches great importance to Stalin's personal contribution to the Anglo-Russian talks. It is said that Eden's impression of the Soviet Russian dictator is that Stalin not only has a thorough observation of international issues, but also has a deep understanding of the characteristics of other countries. This is a fortunate fact, as it can enable Stalin to understand the reasons why Britain cannot be an active participant in the East European security system. The correspondent continued that the statement in the Moscow official newspaper that the purpose of the East European peace organization is not to encircle any country or isolate any country will be welcomed by London. The principles of non-aggression and the loyalty of both countries to the League of Nations mentioned in the official newspaper can be regarded as a symbol of the obvious improvement in diplomatic relations between communist Russia and capitalist Britain. The Daily Mail retaliated with the headline "Anglo-Russian Competition Has Ended" over the news of Eden's departure from Moscow, and stated that after Eden's meetings with Stalin and Litvinov, both sides were surprised that the two countries' views on world issues were so close. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Mutual Recognition of Territorial Integrity: A Striking Statement in the Communique

(Moscow) Soviet Russian officials are extremely satisfied with the results of the talks between the British and Soviet sides. Some sections of the communique issued yesterday exceeded all expectations. For example, the representatives of the two countries expressed their willingness to recognize each other's territorial integrity, which is one of the most striking statements in the communique and was not initially expected. After carefully studying the communique, it can be seen that in the future, it will be Soviet Russia, not Britain, that promotes Germany and Poland's participation in the East European Mutual Assistance Pact. The reason why the Soviet Union was able to achieve success is that the excessive demands made by the German leader Hitler created this opportunity. In short, some people believe that German foreign policy has made mistakes. Eden treated them with sincerity, while Litvinov used his agile skills. Now, looking at Eden's trip, we know that this speculation is not false. A confidant of Eden said, "The field between Britain and Russia has now been cleared, and the sincere cooperation between the two countries has been confirmed." Since the talks in Berlin, the situation has been clarified. It is not difficult for us to predict that as Eden continues his visit to Warsaw, the concept of peace will be flourishing. (Havas dispatch, 1st)

Anglo-Russian Opinions Converge: French Newspapers Express Optimism

(Paris) The newspapers believe that the communique issued after the talks between the British and Soviet ministers is very different in wording from the communique issued after the talks between the British and German ministers. Therefore, they express optimism about the results of the Anglo-Soviet talks. Le Petit Parisien reported, "After the British Lord Privy Seal Eden arrived in Moscow, the Soviet Union warmly welcomed him. The atmosphere of the two talks in Berlin and Moscow and the communiques issued were also different, which shows that Eden's trip was purely exploratory in nature. It has indeed promoted the rapprochement between Britain and the Soviet Union, and also shows that British foreign policy does not allow Germany to be excluded from the Western European powers, but rather draws a line between them." Le Matin commented on the compromise between Britain and the Soviet Union, saying that each country once again applied for German cooperation without hesitation. L'Echo de Paris said, "The communique issued by Moscow is full of enthusiasm in its wording. If we want to understand its profound meaning, we should know that Eden and his interlocutors both attach importance to the Northeast European Mutual Assistance Pact plan. In this way, France does not need to choose a partner between Britain and its allies in Central and Eastern Europe, because Britain and France have the same views on the Northeast European Mutual Assistance Pact plan." Le Journal acknowledged that the wording of the Moscow communique was sincere, but its significance should not be exaggerated, as "its content is not as good as semi-official news. What Britain has done is to let the Soviet Union act on its own, and it remains aloof from the collective security system." Le Figaro said, "If Hitler believes that he can win over Britain to join a crusade against Bolshevism, his views are the same as those of the deposed Emperor Wilhelm II, using fantasies to promote foreign policy." (Havas dispatch, 1st)

Eden Arrives in Warsaw: Meeting with Piłsudski This Morning; Conveying the Results of the German and Russian Talks 86

Warsaw The British Lord Privy Seal Eden, referred to by the local newspapers as one of the most capable young diplomats in the world, will arrive here tonight from Moscow. He originally planned to stay at the British Embassy, but due to the illness of the ambassador, he changed his accommodation to the Hotel Europa. Tomorrow morning, he will meet with Polish Minister of Military Affairs Marshal Piłsudski, known as the "strongman" of Poland, to discuss the overall situation in Europe, and will discuss diplomatic affairs with Foreign Minister Colonel Beck. It is expected that Polish diplomats will not put forward any new proposals, but hope to hear Eden's fair opinions on the results of the talks in Germany and Russia. It is heard that the Polish authorities are prepared to express agreement with any reasonable proposals put forward by Eden. (Reuters dispatch, 1st) After consulting with Marshal Piłsudski and others in Warsaw, Eden plans to go to Prague, the capital of Czechoslovakia, to carry out the final stage of his trip, and then return to London by plane on April 4 to report on his mission. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

Affectionate Farewell to Russia

(Moscow) Eden left here happily tonight for the Polish capital to carry out the third stage of his mission. Before his departure, Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov, British Ambassador Chilston, and other Soviet Russian dignitaries and diplomats were all at the platform to see him off. A red carpet was laid on the platform, and a team of elite Red Army soldiers was lined up. The British and Russian national flags were displayed side by side. Film cameramen recorded this memorable scene. After Eden arrived at the station, he made a speech through a loudspeaker thanking the Soviet Russian government and people for their generous treatment. Litvinov replied, "I wish you success. Your success is our success." Before long, the whistle sounded and the train started moving forward at 10:45 PM. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

Principles of the East European Pact: Poland Still Opposed; Taking the Interests of Western European Powers as Its Own; Determined to Repel the Intrusion of Other Countries' Troops 87

(London) The "News Chronicle" took this opportunity to publish an article written by the London correspondent of the "Warsaw Post," strongly asserting that Poland has always opposed the principles of the multilateral East European Pact. First, it stated, "If Germany develops towards Eastern Europe, it will inevitably encounter Poland's resistance. Some people believe that Poland can obtain assistance from Nazi Germany or Soviet Russia. This statement is not worth the laughter of those in the know, because Poland does not want other countries' troops to enter its territory. Whether it is Germany or Russia, whether it is an allied country or an enemy country, we will not allow its troops to pass through Poland's borders." The conclusion stated, "Poland takes the interests of the Western European powers as its own interests, but the Western European powers should also take the interests of Poland as their own interests." (Havas dispatch, 1st)

Regarding the East European Pact: Britain Has New Proposals; Should Be of the Same Nature as the League of Nations Covenant; Resolutions Should Only Take Effect After Being Passed Unanimously 88

Warsaw The local newspapers received a dispatch from Paris stating that Britain's new proposals regarding the East European Pact have been submitted to the Paris authorities. The British government hopes that the East European Pact should be of the same nature as the League of Nations Covenant, that is, all resolutions should only take effect after being passed unanimously by the signatory countries. The dispatch also stated that this new pact is likely to be accepted unanimously by the countries concerned, allowing them to break away from the current diplomatic deadlock. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Regarding the Far Eastern Security Pact: Japan Expresses Its Attitude; Advocates Setting Up a Demilitarized Zone with Russia First; Then Concluding a Non-Aggression Pact 89

(Tokyo) It is heard that the British representative Eden and the Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov discussed the Far Eastern Locarno Pact. The spokesperson of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs criticized this statement, saying that there is no place like Locarno in the Far East. The changes in the European political situation are extremely frequent and extremely rapid, and are beyond human comprehension. Therefore, the Japanese are not paying attention to Europe now. Before the war, the changes in the European political situation immediately affected the Far East, but this is completely different now. Japan has not received a formal proposal from the Russian government regarding a mutual non-aggression pact. However, the Russian representative in Japan and the Japanese government representative recently exchanged frank opinions on resolving the outstanding issues between the two countries. The Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov once told Japanese journalists that Soviet Russia is prepared to discuss a pact with Japan on mutual non-aggression and not building defensive works. However, Japan believes that before concluding a mutual non-aggression pact, it is necessary to resolve the clause in the Treaty of Portsmouth that does not allow the construction of defensive works, extending it to the Russian "Manchurian" border, in order to eliminate the causes of aggression and abolish the methods of aggression. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

(Tokyo) The Japanese government plans to gradually resolve the diplomatic issues between Japan and the Soviet Union in accordance with the established policy before the start of negotiations on the transfer of the Middle Eastern Railway, and then conclude a non-aggression treaty to establish peaceful relations between the two countries, which is a peaceful adjustment policy for Japanese-Soviet relations. The Soviet Union also wants to conclude a non-aggression treaty as a prerequisite for establishing peaceful cooperation. Recently, Germany recognized the Soviet Union as an enemy of Western European civilization and expressed its absolute opposition to the Soviet Union's participation in the East European Locarno Treaty. This matter caused a major shock to the Soviet leadership, which automatically transferred about half of the 200,000 Red Army soldiers in the Far East to that area to deal with the situation in Eastern Europe. It is believed that the Soviet leadership will propose this issue as a mutual issue, or related to the issue of the demilitarization of the border area between the Soviet Union and "Manchuria" and the issue of a non-aggression treaty. Therefore, the contact between Japan and the Soviet Union following the withdrawal of troops is extremely noteworthy. (Denstu dispatch, 1st)

Japanese and German Militarism: The World War Machine Becomes More Urgent; Moscow Newspapers Publish an Article 90

(Moscow) An article by Bukharin published in Izvestia discusses the issue of peace and the dangerous places in the world. Until recently, there was a dangerous threat of war in the Far East. Japan's aggression against China, its occupation of Manchuria, and its far-reaching plans of conquest (and involving Soviet territory) are the greatest threat to peace. When Bukharin mentioned the war machine in Europe, he pointed out Germany's threats to Memel, Austria, and Lithuania, as well as Hitler's attitude towards the Soviet Union's peaceful policy. Bukharin's militarism: "The Soviet Union never wants war. This is naturally due to its great historical mission. The basic principles and guiding spirit of the Soviet Union's foreign policy are to strive for peace. In our view, since the Soviet Union now represents the interests of 150 million working people and is the most suitable and solid fortress of peace, who can deny that the Soviet Union's cooperation with the bourgeois countries that truly want to maintain peace and whose foreign policy supports the prevention of war is completely in line with its socialist nature? The purpose of the East European Mutual Assistance Pact is to extinguish the fire, and all countries concerned have the opportunity to conclude a pact jointly responsible for the territory of Eastern Europe. Therefore, whether this pact can become a universal agreement for all countries concerned depends entirely on the decision of Germany and Poland." Bukharin concluded, "In the struggle for peace, we should make full use of even the smallest possibility, because this is our historical mission, regardless of whether the provocative forces will implement their policies." (Tass dispatch, 31st)

(Paris) French public opinion attaches great importance to yesterday's talks between Foreign Minister Laval and the British and Russian ambassadors. The talks between Laval and the Russian ambassador were mainly about Laval's visit to Moscow, as the French Foreign Minister plans to visit Russia on April 20, and held preliminary diplomatic talks with the Russian ambassador. The French newspapers, in view of the fact that German leader Hitler has adopted a "completely negative attitude" towards the East European Pact, have unanimously recognized that this is serious and may cause serious political problems, because according to the original plan, Germany's signing was the most important part of the East European Pact plan. Tokyo Port Completed; Took 30 Years; Cost 30 Million 95

(Tokyo) The construction of the Greater Tokyo Port, which took 30 years and cost 33 million yuan, has been completed. The completion ceremony will be held throughout the city today. The ceremony will be held at the work site at the mouth of the Sumida River at 10:00 AM. Prince Hiroyoshi Fushimi will attend. All ships in the port will fly international flags. The construction this time includes the Shibaura pier, which is 1,000 meters long and 8 meters deep nearby. It can moor 7 cargo ships of 7,000 tons. There are now 7 warships moored on the shore for citizens to visit. Ten 3,000-ton ships are docked at the Hinode pier and the Takeshiba pier. Four more piers will be built in the future, which can moor large ships of 8,000 tons. (Nichi-Rengo dispatch, 1st)

Belgian Currency Devaluation Implemented: Authorities Crack Down on Speculation to Prevent Price Hikes 100

Beijing: Today's trading on the Belgian foreign exchange market will be based on a 28% devaluation of the Belgian franc. The Minister of Justice has stated that he will adopt strict measures to crack down on manipulative hoarding. All necessary steps have been taken to prevent price increases. Major domestic stores have pledged full cooperation with the government. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

Beijing: The gold content of the Belgian franc is now set at 0.150632 grams. It is expected that the new value of the Belgian franc will generate high demand for the currency, as the discount on the Belgian franc in foreign markets is between 12% and 15%, while the domestic discount currently reaches 28%. In the past six days, the National Bank of Belgium has lost 350,000,000 francs worth of gold due to gold outflows. The current gold reserve is 56.7%, totaling 11,293,000,000 francs. Going forward, gold reserves will be revalued based on existing reserves. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

Famous American Banker J.P. Morgan Liquidating \$100 Million Fortune: 70% of Assets Converted to Cash to Preserve Financial Power After Death 101

(New York) International banker J.P. Morgan, age 68, is now converting 70% of his assets into cash to pay the state and federal income taxes due after his death. Morgan's assets are estimated to be at least \$100 million. The famous J.P. Morgan Bank has 89 branches, and its total assets were estimated at \$200 million before the economic recession. News that Morgan was aggressively raising cash, even selling his yacht, caused a stir among financiers. It is now confirmed that this move is solely to preserve his financial power after death. Only a small portion of Morgan's assets are in securities that can be readily converted to cash. Morgan now wants to securely pass his bank on to his descendants, so he is converting notes into cash to prepare for contingencies. Recent rumors that Morgan was selling his Long Island property and some of his antiques with the intention of moving to England were dismissed today by Morgan in an interview with the Associated Press. He believes that America has safely emerged from the economic panic, and that inflation is impossible. Morgan then discussed the future of commerce and finance optimistically, stating that the cash he needs now is solely for paying estate taxes, amounting to about 70% of his total assets. The J.P. Morgan Bank will remain under the control of his family. (National Electric dispatch, 31st)

Reorganization in Jiangxi Province: Farmland in Newly Recovered Areas, Agricultural Commission Provides Loans for Resumption of Cultivation; Tenancy Disputes Can Be Resolved Simultaneously 102

Nanchang dispatch: The six counties that were most deeply affected by communist banditry in the past—Ningdu, Ruijin, Huichang, Xingguo, Yudu, and Shicheng—are suffering from chaotic land rights due to the land having been divided up by the bandits. There is also a severe shortage of oxen, farming implements, and seeds. Even those who have land and people are unable to cultivate the land. In light of this, the Provincial Rural Cooperative Committee is using 700,000 yuan in post-disaster fundamental treatment funds to reorganize land rights and boundaries in the aforementioned six counties, and to provide loans for resuming cultivation. The Committee's office in Ningdu has repeatedly consulted with the special commissioners of the twelve districts to implement the allocation of land based on population, in accordance with the land handling regulations promulgated by the Xingying (Military Affairs Commission). Each county has also convened district and baojia (local administrative units) chiefs to discuss the implementation steps, ensuring that there are people to cultivate the land and that there is land for people to cultivate, avoiding renewed tenancy disputes or mutual hesitation. Every able-bodied man in the bandit areas can receive a certain amount of land, and then they can use cooperation to supply oxen, farming implements, and seeds to resume cultivation. (March 24th)

Southwestern Aviation Civil Aviation Aircraft "Changgeng" Crashes into River in Wuzhou: Pilot and Passengers Injured and Rescued, Entire Aircraft Sinks and is Being Salvaged 103

Guangzhou dispatch: The Guangdong-Guangxi Southwestern Civil Aviation Company operates regular civil aviation flights between Longzhou and Guangzhou, transporting passengers and mail. On the 22nd of this month, the company's civil aviation aircraft "Changgeng" was flying east from Longzhou back to Guangdong, piloted by pilot Feng Xinghang. The aircraft departed from Longzhou on the morning of that day and arrived in Nanning at around 11:00 a.m. After unloading mail and cargo, three passengers boarded: a German, Yu Changju, the South China manager of the Xintong Trading Company, and Qiu Guozhen, a colonel staff officer of the Guangxi Army Headquarters. It departed from Nanning and arrived in Wuzhou at 1:00 p.m., landing at the Gaowang Airport across the river from Wuzhou. As usual, there was a brief stop in Wuzhou, and the pilot and passengers had lunch together. The company's Wuzhou station staff also loaded newspapers and mail onto the aircraft, along with some light goods. At 3:15 p.m., after everything was prepared, it took off for Guangdong. Prior to departure, the pilot inspected the aircraft's components and added fuel. As it soared upwards and circled once, intending to head east, the aircraft suddenly emitted sparks from the engine about two minutes after leaving the airport, accompanied by a loud noise. The pilot knew something was wrong and quickly steered the aircraft towards the river, causing it to crash into the water. However, the engine had already failed, and at 3:25 p.m., the entire aircraft descended vertically, plunging into the water, causing water to splash in all directions and creating a large white wave. The passengers inside the aircraft knew there was no escape. The German was the first to break through the glass door and escape. Pilot Feng Xinghang also risked his life to get out. The two passengers in the back seat, Yu and Qiu, clung to the aircraft's wings, floating on the surface of the water, and shouted for help. The Wuzhou station staff of the civil aviation company, hearing the alarm, immediately sent a boat to rescue them. A Mobil Oil Company gasoline boat nearby arrived first and rescued the pilot and three passengers, sending them back to Wuzhou City, where they were settled separately. Among the passengers, only the German suffered minor head injuries. Pilot Feng Xinghang suffered no major injuries to his hands and feet. Although passengers Qiu and Yu had a scare, they were unharmed and took a civilian ship back to Guangdong that night. The mail and goods carried on the "Changgeng" aircraft were lost to the east, and after the entire aircraft sank, it is not known where it drifted. The Wuzhou station staff are currently trying to salvage it. It is said that the loss from this aircraft accident is no less than 200,000 yuan. (March 27th)

Regiment Commander Yuan Jin of the 9th Division Dishonored the Reputation of the Revolutionary Army: Executed by Firing Squad on the Order of Chairman Chiang 104

Xiamen dispatch: Yuan Jin, the deputy regiment commander of the supplementary regiment of the 9th Division stationed in Zhangzhou, and Dan Da, the third battalion commander, were detained by Division Commander Li Yannian for condoning drug offenders. They were subsequently ordered to be executed by firing squad in Zhangzhou on March 30th. The Southwest Pacification Headquarters announced the crimes of Yuan and Dan, as follows: "According to Chairman Chiang's confidential telegram from Chongqing, Li, Division Commander Yannian, reported that Yuan Jin, the acting regiment commander of the supplementary regiment of my division, and Dan Da, the third battalion commander of the regiment, were found to have violated laws and condoned drug offenders in the locality. After investigation, the facts were confirmed. It is proposed that the officers be dismissed and sentenced to imprisonment for more than two years as a warning. In addition to submitting the entire case file along with the verdict, I hereby telegraph to request instructions. After investigation, Yuan Jin and Dan Da were found to have condoned drug offenders. The said Yuan Jin and Dan Da were found to have condoned drug offenses and have been found guilty by the divisional commander in charge. It is clear that there is no doubt that they have dishonored the reputation of the Revolutionary Army. They should be interrogated and executed on the spot without delay. A report should be made. It was ordered that the two officials, Yuan Jin and Dan Da, be sent to the headquarters by the said divisional commander. After interrogation, it was confirmed that they had jointly bribed Cai Wenhua, a morphine trafficker from Shishi, and forced Wu Shigu, a sugar dealer in the area, to sell smuggled sugar without paying taxes, and divided the proceeds. Therefore, in compliance with the telegram and in accordance with Article 1, Section 2 of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Criminal Law, and Articles 7 and 10 of the Provisional Regulations for the Strict Prohibition of Potent Drugs, the two criminals, Yuan Jin and Dan Da, were identified on this day and executed by firing squad at the execution ground to maintain military discipline and as a solemn warning. This announcement lists one official, Yuan Jin, age 26, from Rucheng County, Hunan Province, formerly the regiment commander of the supplementary regiment of the 9th Division of the Army; and Dan Da, age 33, from Huangmei County, Hubei Province, formerly the third battalion commander of the supplementary regiment of the 9th Division of the Army." (31st)

Revocation of Land Grant for Confucian Temple 107

The land on which the Confucian temple in this county is located was previously granted to local residents by the Office of Public Property, causing surprise among the local populace. In November of the 22nd year of the Republic [1933], the county government submitted a request to the provincial government, which issued Directive No. 25 of the Finance Department, approving the revocation of the land grant, refunding the original price, canceling the ministerial certificate, and ordering the Bureau of Education to take back possession and safeguard the property, while also informing the Office of Public Property for compliance. More than a year has passed, but the land recipients have not yet complied. The Mountain Bureau of Education requested instructions from the county government. Now, the Office of Public Property has reported that the recipients of the land grant for the government's Confucian temple are Wang Sanhuai, Yu Jisheng, Ye Genzhu, and Jin Rong; and the recipients of the county's Confucian temple land grant are the Yin family, Chen Zujian, Hongde, and Zhang Zuoji. The head patrol officer of the First Precinct, Lu Jianfen, has been ordered to summon them to the Shatianzhu Bureau to receive the refund and surrender their certificates to resolve the outstanding case.

Qingpu: Dispute During Party Headquarters' Joint Commemoration Week 108

The County Party Headquarters held a joint commemoration week yesterday. Because the representatives from various district branch offices raised questions about party affairs, they posed several questions to the chairman, who was unable to answer them, arousing public anger and leading to a dispute. A detailed account is presented to the provincial government for review, as follows: The Qingpu County Party Headquarters held a joint commemoration week yesterday morning at 9:00 a.m. In addition to the participation of the city, Chairman Cheng Sinong performed the rituals. After the chairman finished his report, various points of contention were raised, with questions posed: (1) The Xicen Book and Newspaper Agency, established by the County Party Headquarters, was previously opposed, so why was it suddenly reopened? (2) Zai Diren lives in Huangdu and works primarily in Huangdu, so why is his party membership in Baihejiang? (3) There is solid evidence that Wu Changqi of the tax collection office embezzled public funds, so why did the Party newspaper initially strongly condemn him and then ignore the issue? (4) When a refugee disturbance occurred in Yangdian Village in the second district, why did the County Party Headquarters not pay attention to it before the issue was resolved? (5) Why can prospective party members be entirely controlled by Standing Committee member Huang Xuze personally, who even fabricates forms on his own? (6) Regarding the Huangdu rice robbery and the Qingpu Entertainment Center brawl last year, why were they not disclosed in the Party newspaper because they were unfavorable to Huang Xuze? At the time, the chairman was unable to answer any of the questions. Comrades demanded that Huang Xuze, a Standing Committee member of the County Party Headquarters, be personally responsible for answering them. However, Huang was in Huangdu on private business and had not returned, so Chairman Cheng Sinong could not provide answers, and attempted to declare the ceremony completed and dismiss the meeting. This agitated the public, causing a dispute.

Serial Robbery and Murder Cases Occur in Villages 110

Two bandit boats carrying more than twenty bandits arrived at Ruomao浜 in Zhouzhuang Township the night before last, robbing more than ten households, resulting in losses of over a thousand taels of silver. They then went to Zhujiahe Village and robbed seven households, including Shen Luming's, resulting in losses of approximately five to six thousand taels of silver. Furthermore, Yang Laotai and more than twenty others from Xiatang in Qimen hired a boat to Hangzhou to offer incense. While passing near Pingwang, they were robbed by bandits, and all the incense worshippers were searched, none spared, with losses of five to six hundred yuan. Also, on the night of the 29th, more than ten bandits arrived at the home of a farmer surnamed Sun in Tuncun, Wujiang County. They tied up Sun and shot him in the foot. As Sun struggled, the bandits fired another shot, which unfortunately hit a vital spot, resulting in his death. After receiving reports from the victims and various squads, Zhou, the chief of the 2nd waterway police district, immediately ordered his subordinates yesterday (the 1st) to strictly investigate and arrest the perpetrators.

Wuxi: Two Youths Arrested for Investigating Commercial Fraud 111

Two youths from Ningbo, Tan Zuyin and Tan Mengming, came to Wuxi in winter, carrying a survey book. They went to various merchants inside and outside the city, claiming to be from the Shanghai Commercial Advertising Agency, coming to Wuxi to conduct commercial surveys, with no other purpose. They recorded the name, address, telephone number, and manager's name of each store in the book, and instructed each store to affix a seal in the book. At the time, the stores did not suspect anything. Recently, the Tans suddenly came to Wuxi again, still carrying the same survey book. However, next to the seals of each merchant in the book, the words "Attention: Publication Fee of One Yuan, Payable After Publication" had been added. They also carried a commercial directory containing the names of stores in Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and other places, totaling over ten thousand households. They went door-to-door to the merchants they had surveyed last year, collecting an advertising fee of one yuan. The stores, realizing that they had claimed to be conducting commercial surveys last year but were now suddenly collecting publication fees, suspected that they were fraudulently obtaining money and reported them to the police. The police took them to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Many of the defrauded merchants went to the bureau to report them. After Officer Min opened court and questioned them, the Tans confessed that they had only printed one copy of the commercial directory and were evasive about other matters. They only wanted to refund the publication fees they had collected. Officer Min, considering that the case involved fraud, deemed it inappropriate to release them lightly and immediately sent them to the General Bureau for interrogation and detention, awaiting transfer to the court for legal proceedings.

Haimen: Gu Fengchao Escorted to Shanghai for Trial 112

Gu Fengchao, the director of the Qidong Tooth Tax Collection Office, was accused of extortion and harassment of merchants and residents. The case was brought to the Nantong Regional Commissioner's Office. Commissioner Zheng sent personnel to investigate and confirmed the facts. He ordered the Qidong County Government to dismiss and detain Gu. Subsequently, Gu applied to the High Court for a change of jurisdiction. The High Court designated the Shanghai District Court to hear the case. Yesterday, the Qidong County Government sent police to escort Gu to the Shanghai District Court for trial.

County Government Requests Opening of Brothels 113

Since the explicit prohibition of prostitution in this county, although public prostitutes have gradually decreased, the number of secret private prostitutes has suddenly increased. According to recent statistics from various hospitals, a large number of patients are suffering from gonorrhea, syphilis, and other diseases. It is believed that the cause is the spread by private prostitutes. In light of this, the county government has drafted regulations for the management of prostitutes, allowing them to pay monthly donations to operate, designating doctors to examine their bodies once a week, and ordering those with diseases to seek treatment to prevent transmission. The regulations also prescribe attire to prevent them from mingling with respectable women. Yesterday (the 30th), the detailed regulations were submitted to the Civil Affairs Department for review. Once approved, they can be implemented.

Yangzhou: Buddhist Association Allocates Disaster Relief Based on Mu 114

The Jiangdu County Government is facing a shortage of funds for purchasing rice and providing seeds for the disaster areas of the eighth and ninth districts. It has allocated 2,000 yuan to be raised by the Jiangdu Buddhist Association. The association has now convened the abbots of temples in urban and rural areas to discuss a solution. It has been decided that the amount to be donated will be based on the amount of temple-owned farmland, with the amount to be raised calculated on a per-mu basis. The amount to be donated will be calculated in the following way: farmland in disaster areas is excluded; for temples with less than 500 mu of land, each mu will donate 1 jiao of silver; for temples with more than 500 mu, each mu will donate 8 fen of silver; temples with no farmland and retired monks will be solicited by the association through Jian Cheng, Songshan, Mo Zhi, Wei Jing, Miao Ji, Xin Tan, and Ai Dao Tang, who will carry donation books and collect the pledged donations. The deadline for collecting the donations and submitting them to the association is April 7th, so that they can be forwarded to the county. Contributions may also be solicited from donors to the best of their ability and submitted together.

They have now formed a ferry service to benefit travelers and requested that it be registered. Jiaoxi Town in Wujin has never had a post office, only an agency. Cao Bingkang, the chief of the sub-bureau, has been appointed by the General Bureau to fill the post. It was implemented on April 1st.

Huaiyin: Repairing the Yangzhuang Dam 119

Yangzhuang in this district is the starting section for diverting the Huai River into the sea. [Text missing.] To the west is where the water of the Huai River is stored. If the dam is damaged, it will inevitably affect the downstream Huai River diversion project. The Engineering Office reported that the dam was in disrepair. Not only would this affect the upcoming flood season, but its height would not be sufficient to protect the project. Therefore, on the 30th, the office dispatched Wang Mengzhou, the director of the construction section, and Zhu Gongshuo, the head of the materials section, to assess the situation and make preparations for construction to begin on a selected date.

Lianshui: County Magistrate Shen Pays Attention to the Huai River Diversion Project 120

Lianshui is located in the center of the Huai River Diversion Project and its engineering is extremely important. Therefore, County Magistrate Shen Jinghua does not dare to neglect any of the project sections within the county's borders. It was recently reported that there were instances of laziness and gambling among the workers in the Diàn湖 area east of the county. This not only hinders the progress of the project but also causes disputes. In addition to immediately ordering strict prohibition, he personally went to the Diàn湖 construction area to inspect and supervise the soil removal work. He visited on the 25th and only returned yesterday. Furthermore, various Huai River diversion project markers in Lianshui are often mistakenly pulled out by farmers due to the vastness of the land and the difficulty of taking care of them, which hinders the project. Yesterday, each section reported this problem, and a notice was issued simultaneously to prohibit it. In the future, anyone who damages the markers will be punished accordingly without leniency.

Gaoyou: Chamber of Commerce Plans to Raise Funds to Help Disaster Victims in Caojiaqiao 121

The seventh and eighth districts of this county in the west of the lake suffered a drought last year, resulting in a complete crop failure. Most of the farmers in the area have taken their elderly and young children to neighboring counties to beg for food. The situation is especially dire in the Caojiaqiao area of the seventh district. With the spring famine approaching, the strong have gone out to seek a living, while the elderly and weak stay at home, grinding tree bark and grass to fill their stomachs. Upon learning of the disaster situation in the area, Wang Hongzao, chairman of the county chamber of commerce, and Liu Lingsheng, a philanthropist from Yangzhou, plan to raise funds to purchase flour and request the county government to send personnel to distribute it together, and to collect relief funds for distribution to benefit the disaster-stricken people.

Jiashan: Robbery of More Than Twenty Homes in Sanbaitang 122

Sanbaitang in the northern countryside has long been a place where bandits appear and ships are often harmed. Recently, a large gang of bandits has been lurking there. At 8:00 p.m. the night before last, more than ten bandits armed with knives and clubs went to the Jiangjiawan area on the edge of the Tang, robbing seven households, including Gu Jinxiang's. The stolen clothing, ornaments, and silver dollars were quite large in number. At midnight, they went to the Tujiazha area and robbed about fourteen or fifteen households, causing losses of tens of thousands of dollars. Liu Rouquan, the leader of the third squad of the water patrol, dispatched a squad to pursue and suppress them after receiving the report. It is reported that there was a fierce battle.

Jiaxing: County Government Abolishes Bureaus and Manages Departments 123

The Jiaxing County Government was ordered to pilot the abolition of bureaus and change to departments. Each bureau was closed at the end of March and the change to departments took effect on April 1st. County Magistrate Wang Xianqiang has assigned Secretary Zhu Yisheng to take over the Construction Department, Xie Ruchang to take over the Education Bureau, Second Department Chief Zhang Haoming to take over the Finance Bureau, and Li Yuan to take over the Public Security Bureau. After the bureaus are changed to departments, there will be a large number of personnel changes. All the dismissed officials will be given a month's severance pay by the county, with the approval of the province, to allow them to return to their hometowns. The Construction Department will move into the Finance Department, and the Public Security Department will move into the original site of the Construction Department. The Public Security Bureau will be changed to a branch, with the department chief Li Yuan concurrently serving as the director.

Xiaoshan: Gang of Thieves Sentenced to Ten Years in Prison 124

On February 25th of this year, the home of Ni Shaoting, a resident of Xinxia in Yiqiao, Xiaoshan, was broken into by nine bandits who ransacked the place, stealing two boxes of leather clothing and one box of pearls and gold jewelry, worth more than 2,500 taels of silver. The Yiqiao Public Security Sub-bureau arrested two thieves, Ni Xiaojinsheng and Ni Ahu. The other seven are still at large. The County Court first opened court and interrogated the two thieves twice. On the 28th, it appointed lawyers Yu Xuesong and Wang Yumo to appear in court for defense. After the debate concluded, they were sentenced to ten years in prison the next day.

Implementing Land Survey Public Bond Allocation 125

Due to the shortage of funds for land surveying in Xiaoshan, the provincial government was specially approved to issue short-term public bonds. A total of 200,000 yuan was issued in the county, of which 50,000 yuan was allocated to the urban area and the remaining 50,000 yuan each to the southern, western, and eastern rural areas. The funds will be paid in two installments from April to August. In addition to appointing township chiefs, county councilors, and parliament members as responsible fund-raising personnel, standing committee members for public bond management are publicly elected in each township to take charge of their duties.

Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Held Sanitation Campaign Yesterday; Posters Displayed at Stations and Propaganda Train Launched; Deputy Director Wu Expresses Significance of Sanitation Campaign 130

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Bureau, in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Railways, held a sanitation campaign on the entire line yesterday (April 1st). The national flag was hung at the North Station and stations along the two lines. Sanitation charts were displayed inside the stations, and a propaganda train was launched for publicity. The reporter from Shenshi News Agency learned the details and described them as follows:

Held on the Entire Line Yesterday

The Railways Bureau, in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Railways, held the second sanitation campaign yesterday (the first was held last year). The national flag was hung at the gate of the North Station, along with a white banner that read "Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Sanitation Campaign." All stations along the line were similarly decorated. Various sanitation charts and propaganda texts were posted inside the stations. Each major station sent propagandists to give speeches, and three propaganda trains were attached to the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou passenger trains for onboard publicity. In addition, the Preparatory Committee's Health and Cleaning Groups sent personnel to carry out tasks such as vaccination and cleaning.

Deputy Director Wu's Opinion

Wu Shaozeng, Deputy Director of the Bureau, expressed his views on the sanitation campaign yesterday, saying, "Our railway follows the orders of the Ministry of Railways and holds a sanitation campaign every year. The purpose is nothing more than two points: (1) A sound mind often resides in a sound body, and the success of work is often directly proportional to the vigor of the spirit. This is an immutable principle. Our staff serving in the railway have heavy responsibilities. If their bodies are not healthy, they will not only be unable to perform their duties happily, but also inevitably delay opportunities and cause accidents, resulting in a major blow to the business. To make the body healthy, paying attention to hygiene is a necessary path. Therefore, when we hold the sanitation campaign, internally, we make all employees pay attention to hygiene, improve their health, and thus improve work efficiency. (2) Trains come and go, and there are many passengers. If the stations, vehicles, and all traffic equipment are not kept tidy and clean, it will not only be unsightly but also inevitably leave various adverse effects on the physical and mental health of passengers. Therefore, when we hold the sanitation campaign, externally, we want to make all railway employees keep all traffic equipment clean and tidy at all times and places, thereby maintaining passenger safety and increasing common enjoyment."

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Purchases Freighter, Named "Dafei", Expected to Arrive in Shanghai by the End of the Month 134

The state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, due to business development and cooperation with the Ministry of Railways in handling national intermodal transport, felt that there were not enough ships to allocate. Therefore, it purchased a freighter, which has been completed and is expected to be delivered by the end of this month. The reporter from the Central News Agency learned the details as follows:

Arriving in Shanghai by the End of the Month: In order to manage various routes, the Bureau purchased a freighter built in 1910 from the French shipping management company with the surplus and remaining funds from the purchase of materials in recent months. The Ministry of Communications approved it early on. At the end of June this year, the company sent personnel to the Rhine River to pick it up, stating that the delivery would be in Shanghai and a partial deposit would be paid first. Since the ship involves manufacturing, subleasing, berthing, and other aspects of several countries, it is necessary to complete all the formalities. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai by the end of this month.

Named Dafei: It has been decided to name the ship Dafei. It has a total tonnage of 5,620 tons, a net tonnage of 4,070 tons, a length of 340 feet, and a speed of 11 nautical miles per hour. The purchase price is several thousand British pounds. In the future, it is planned to sail between Shanghai and Haizhou, connecting with the Longhai Railway, specializing in intermodal transport goods, because the ship is a pure freighter. It is rumored that the Bureau plans to purchase a large number of ships. According to the person in charge of the Bureau, the Central News Agency reporter said that there are indeed many people who come to solicit business, but the Bureau is limited by economics and it is difficult to realize.

Financial Bonds Issued Yesterday: Three Banks Increase Capital for Interbank Lending to Rescue the Market; Commercial Acceptance Bills Begin Yesterday; Credit Lending Syndicate to Be Established Soon 135

According to Xinsheng News Agency, the Republic of China 24th Year Financial Bonds to rescue the market were issued yesterday. The Silk and Satin Trades Association and Silk Weaving Trade Association pioneered commercial acceptance bills, which were also implemented yesterday. The Industrial and Commercial Credit Small Lending Syndicate will be established soon. After the three banks increased their capital, they made large interbank loans to rescue the market. The details are as follows:

Financial Bonds Issued Yesterday

In order to enrich the capital of the Central Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, repay advances, consolidate finance, and facilitate the rescue of industry and commerce, the Ministry of Finance issued 10 million yuan of the Republic of China 24th Year Financial Bonds, which were issued at face value yesterday. Subscription warrants have been printed. After the bonds are printed, they will be exchanged. The annual interest rate is 6%, and the principal and interest will be fully repaid by March 31 of the 34th year of the Republic of China. The Central Bank, the China Bank, and the Bank of Communications are designated as the principal and interest management agencies, and the newly added tariff is designated as the fund.

Lending Syndicate to Be Established Soon

The Industrial and Commercial Credit Small Lending Plan of 5 million yuan to rescue the market, the member banks of the Banking Association have raised 2.5 million yuan, and the government's 2.5 million yuan is borne by the Central Bank, jointly forming the Industrial and Commercial Credit Small Lending Syndicate to handle it. Everything is now ready. After the Central Bank receives the order, it will be implemented immediately. Due to the China Bank issue in recent days, it has been slightly delayed. Now, Song Hanzhang has taken over as the General Manager of the China Bank, so the establishment date of the syndicate will not be far away.

Commercial Acceptance Bills Implemented

The Silk and Satin Trades Association and Silk Weaving Trade Association pioneered commercial acceptance bills, which were implemented yesterday. The Shanghai Silk Industry Bank has agreed to handle discounting. At the same time, the Central Bank has agreed to handle re-discounting. All procedures, bill styles, etc., have been reported in the newspapers. The various out-of-town merchant groups, after economic experts Zhang Naiqi, Jin Guobao, Li Quanshi, etc., and Chairman Luo Qinghua gave detailed explanations at the banquet of the two trade associations the night before, have fully understood. It was first implemented yesterday, and there were no difficulties.

Three Banks Interbank Lending to Rescue the Market

After the Central Bank of China and the Bank of Communications designated large sums for interbank lending to the banking and money industries in order to regulate finance, although directly to the banking and money industries, and indirectly to industry and commerce, after the Ministry of Finance allocated the 24th Year Financial Bonds to enrich the capital of the three banks, the bonds were issued yesterday. From now on, the capital of the three banks will be more consolidated. Therefore, after consultation, the three banks decided to expand the interbank lending to the banking and money industries.

German Express Mail Ship "Cardillera" Arrives Today, Set to Spark Competition Among Foreign Steamships 138

The German HAPAG liner "Cardillera" of the Hamburg-America Line, departed from Germany on February 23rd for Shanghai. All passenger cabins were fully booked. This ship is one of the four newly added express mail ships of Germany, with a deadweight of 16,000 tons, 159 first-class cabins, 100 second-class cabins, and 110 third-class cabins. The company received a telegram yesterday from the shipowner C. D'Ottilie, stating that the ship is scheduled to enter port at 10:00 AM today, and berth at the Jardine Matheson Wharf at 11:30 AM. Therefore, the company has hired a pilot to guide the ship into port and is scheduled to depart for Japan on the 5th, and return to Shanghai on the 16th before heading back to Europe.

Full of Passengers

Among those arriving in Shanghai on this ship from Europe, 130 will disembark in Shanghai. Among the passengers is the Chinese Central Government's Minister TzeKing Ouei, along with his wife, son, and entourage, returning to the country. They will disembark at the Jardine Matheson Wharf at 11:40 AM today. As for passengers going to Europe, their tickets were fully booked a month ago. According to the company's information, the ship's round-trip passenger ticket revenue to the Far East alone amounts to approximately 600,000 Chinese national currency. Adding freight charges, the amount is considerable. The round trip takes a total of 90 days, returning to Hamburg on May 23rd.

"Cardillera"

North German Lloyd Agency

The original plan of HAPAG was to dispatch two special express liners each with North German Lloyd. Those dispatched by HAPAG were the "Cardillera" and "Boschdyk," while those dispatched by North German Lloyd were the "Scharnhorst" and "Gneisenau." The two companies were to operate separate schedules. After the "Cardillera" arrived, it was originally planned to invite people from all walks of life in Shanghai to visit the ship, with the company hosting. However, following an order from the German government, the HAPAG express liners were placed under the agency of North German Lloyd, to avoid competition between two German companies on the same route. Therefore, the plan was changed, and HAPAG ships were handed over to North German Lloyd for scheduling. Thus, the invitation to the "Cardillera" to the Shanghai public for a tour was cancelled.

Competition Among Foreign Steamships

North German Lloyd's first new ship, the "Scharnhorst," is scheduled to make its maiden voyage to Shanghai on the 8th of next month. Due to the exchange rate between China and Germany, the ticket prices for German express liners are cheaper compared to those of other countries. Therefore, representatives from the Japan Mail Line, Osaka Shosen Kaisha, Pacific Mail Steamship Company, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Dollar Steamship Lines, and American Mail Line, including Huis, Meduna, Bacon, and Clark, held a general meeting at the China Merchants company. They agreed to dissolve the passenger ticket alliance between Europe and the Far East with immediate effect, preparing to compete with German ships by lowering prices. Therefore, from the date of the "Scharnhorst's" maiden voyage, an unprecedented competition will be triggered on the China-Europe route.

The Shanghai City Recruitment Team Office of the China Aviation Association held its sixth office meeting at the office yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM to discuss future direction. Attendees included Chief Secretary Li Dachao, Secretaries Zhang Yuliang, Gu Shangrui, Zhu Shengyang, Li Wenyue, Zhou Xin, Xue Baolun, Lu Zhangyan, Li Jimin, Song Zheng, Zhou Songhe, Chen Shuo, Liu Songtao, and others. Li Dachao chaired the meeting and Chen Shuo recorded the minutes. The chairman reported that since the commencement of the second recruitment campaign, the teams have been working diligently, and we should do our best to assist their progress to reach the target of recruiting 100,000 members and raising 1 million yuan for aviation to save the country. The teams have already appointed deputy team leaders and members and should be in contact with them to encourage their efforts. In addition, the office has been collecting aviation donations from various industries throughout the city, and each industry has enthusiastically supported it. For example, the freight trucking industry has already passed a resolution to collect 100,000 yuan, and the brick and tile transportation industry has also tentatively decided to collect 20,000 yuan. The principle of utilizing waste cigarette packs for aviation donations has been approved by the cigarette industry association, and the specific measures are being drafted and will be implemented soon. Recently, the collection of aviation donations from the restaurant and food industry has been scheduled for the 3rd of this month, when a meeting will be convened with various restaurants and food establishments to discuss its implementation. Subsequently, the meeting discussed various issues related to fundraising and recruitment, as well as the speedy preparation for the Boy Scouts mobilization for recruitment. Starting today, the office will directly solicit memberships and raise funds for aviation to save the country.

Since the General Team Office began recruiting group members, various organizations and groups have enthusiastically joined. As reported earlier, the Shanghai Copper, Iron, and Machinery Industry Association submitted their membership application and membership fee of 50 yuan yesterday. Shen Jun, the captain of Team 320 and principal of Yunzhong Girls' Middle School, is making great efforts in the recruitment work. It is reported that he has expanded the recruitment to all teachers and students of the school, encouraging them to join the China Aviation Association as members. He has also stipulated that all teachers and students of the school must be responsible for recruitment work and solicit family members of students to become members, as well as raising funds for aviation to save the country. Yang Hu, the captain of Team 146, and Zhu Wenqi, the captain of Team 3, are making great efforts in recruitment, resulting in a shortage of various recruitment documents previously issued. They have requested the continued issuance of several hundred copies of various promotional materials, membership applications, and badges. It is reported that the General Team Office has sent them separately, demonstrating the enthusiasm of the team leaders for the work and the general support for aviation.

The Two Railway Bureaus Held a Farewell Banquet for the Outgoing Chief of the Accounting Department Yesterday, and Welcomed the Newly Appointed Chief 145

Lankester, Chief of the Accounting Department of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, was reinstated in mid-March of last year after the resignation of Sir Revis. He requested a one-year term, which was approved by the Ministry of Railways. At the same time, the Ministry negotiated with the Sino-British Bank to determine the successor. It was decided that Mr. Stewart would take over. Mr. Stewart arrived in the bureau in January of this year and was first assigned as an accounting specialist, serving in the Accounting Department to familiarize himself with the accounting situation of the bureau. Now, Mr. Lankester will relinquish his duties as Chief of the Accounting Department on April 1st, and Mr. Stewart will take over as Chief of the Accounting Department from that day. Mr. Lankester initially arrived at the railway on March 19, 1908, as the Director of the Passenger and Freight Section of the Accounting Department. He resigned on April 30, 1914. On December 16 of the same year, he was re-engaged by the railway and appointed as Deputy Chief Accountant. At the end of June 1923, the original Chief Accountant, Mr. Middleton, resigned and returned to England, and Mr. Lankester was promoted to fill the vacancy. He resigned again on April 30, 1931. His successor as Chief of the Accounting Department was Sir Revis. Before long, Sir Revis also resigned due to old age and weakness. Mr. Lankester was re-engaged by the bureau for the third time on March 23 of last year, resuming his original position as Chief of the Accounting Department. The bureau reported to the Ministry of Railways that Mr. Lankester had served in the bureau for a total of eleven and a half years and had made significant contributions. The Ministry of Railways awarded him a certificate of commendation. As he had to return to his country after his resignation, a farewell banquet was held at the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road at noon yesterday, and Mr. Stewart was welcomed. The Chief Auditor, Secretary, and leaders of various departments were invited to accompany them. During the banquet, Deputy Director Wu of the bureau delivered a farewell speech, recounting Mr. Lankester's history of service on the railway and wishing him a successful retirement. He then reported on the experience of the newly appointed Chief, Mr. Stewart, as an introduction, and hoped that he would have the same long service and remarkable achievements as Mr. Lankester. Mr. Lankester delivered a reply, expressing his regret at leaving the railway, which he had served for nearly a quarter of a century, and wishing that even though their physical forms would be separated in the future, their spirits would remain connected. Mr. Stewart also delivered a reply, expressing his willingness to contribute his full enthusiasm and best efforts to the national railways of the Republic of China and provide the best service. Mr. Stewart was originally an accountant in England. In 1923, he went to India and worked at the Lovelock and Leweo accounting firm in Calcutta, specializing in auditing the accounts of railways, trams, electric lights, and coal mines for ten years.

Former British Judge Wilkinson Passed Away Yesterday 146

According to the Da Mei Evening News, Mr. Wilkinson, a former British Royal Counsel in China who served as the Chief Justice of the High Court of Weihaiwei, suddenly suffered from pneumonia a few days ago and was admitted to the Hong'en Hospital for treatment. He passed away in the hospital today (the 1st). Mr. Wilkinson was the eldest son of the late Sir Hiram Wilkinson, British Assessor for Japan and Korea in China. He was born in 1866 and was well-versed in law. After coming to China, he engaged in legal practice and served as a British Royal Counsel for many years, handling several major cases. In 1926, he retired and returned to his hometown in Ireland. Three or four years ago, he returned to China to settle some inheritance left by his father in the Zhabei district. He had extensive social interactions with Chinese and foreigners in Shanghai and wrote several books. His wife lives in Hong Kong and sent a telegram last week asking him to come to Shanghai, but he only boarded the ship on Saturday and is still on the way.

The Hamburg-America Line's round-the-world cruise ship, the Resolute, carrying over 300 tourists, departed from New York, USA on January 12, traveling to major commercial ports around the world. It has passed Hong Kong and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at around 3:00 AM tomorrow morning (the 3rd), berthing at the Jardine Matheson Wharf in Hongkou. It is scheduled to stay in Shanghai for one day and then go north to Qinhuangdao, then travel to Beijing. The ship weighs 20,000 tons, is a motor ship, 620 feet long and 72 feet wide. The ship plans to visit a total of 76 commercial ports. There are four distinguished guests among the passengers, one being the Prince and Princess of Hohenlohe-Langenburg of Germany, and the other being the Prince and Princess of Schaumburg-Lippe of Germany. They will arrive in Shanghai on the same ship on that day. After arriving in Shanghai, the passengers will visit Nanshi, Longhua, and other places. In the afternoon, they will visit the City God Temple. They will then board the ship in the evening and leave Shanghai at 8:00 AM the next morning to continue their journey.

Li Mingyu's Family Entrusted Lawyers to Negotiate with the French Consul-General Regarding His Arrest, The French Consul-General Agreed to Investigate, If Indeed Naturalized as Chinese, He Should Be Protected 148

According to the Xin Li News Agency, Korean Cui Yingxin (i.e., Li Mingyu) was arrested by the French Municipal Police at 7:00 AM on March 26 of this year at Xiecheng Lane, Rue Pére Robert. It has been found that Cui Yingxin was naturalized as Chinese on June 13, 1925, and has worked as a ticket collector at the Shanghai British Tramway Company for many years. He later engaged in the ginseng business and has always been law-abiding. Cui Yingxin's wife believes that since her husband has been naturalized as Chinese, he should be tried by the Chinese court, regardless of whether he is suspected of committing a crime. She entrusted lawyers Lou Yunmei and Xu Jie to visit the French Municipal Police and request the French Consul-General. There was no definite indication. Yesterday, they visited the French Consul-General on Rue de Consulat. Consul-General Bellion received them. He stated that he was not aware of the matter and had not signed the warrant for Cui Yingxin's arrest. After lawyers Lou and Xu explained the details of the arrest, the French Consul-General agreed to investigate and stated that if he had indeed been naturalized as Chinese, he should be protected according to the law. It has also been found that Cui Yingxin's naturalization certificate was seized by the French Municipal Police that day. Therefore, the family only knows the date of naturalization and cannot remember the number listed on the certificate. For the convenience of negotiation, Lawyer Lou and others have telegraphed the Ministry of Interior to provide a certified copy of Cui's naturalization process and requested that it be transferred to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a protest. They have also sent letters to the Shanghai Bar Association requesting assistance.
